            Thought for 9m 23s
            I read the uploaded draft as a hostile referee would. The strongest defensible core is
            much narrower than the current framing: you have a formal algebraic PBW-shadow
            theorem for a selected stable trace sector, plus a degree-zero Hamiltonian Poisson
            trace map. You do not yet have a closed-open string theorem, a cochain-level
            factorization-center map, or a deformation-level cotangent/descendant match.

            The paper itself states that the identification is “a filtered graded-commutative PBW
            special-fibre product identification, not a deformation-level identification of the
            descendant module actions.” That is a major downgrade, not a technical caveat. It
            means the open algebra is not shown to be the Koszul dual of the closed algebra; it is
            shown to match the associated graded commutative shadow of that Koszul dual, and
            only in a selected sector. main
            So the theorem title “Local stable Hamiltonian-sector Koszul duality” is too strong. A
            more honest title would be:
                PBW special-fibre comparison for the stable Hamiltonian trace sector.
            If you keep the current title, a referee can fairly say the title claims a deformation-level
            Koszul duality theorem that the body explicitly disclaims.

            3. The cotangent/descendant sector does not match the closed BF
            module
            The closed Lie algebra is

                                               1 2

            Even the direction is wrong in the simplest case: z1 lowers the open descendant index b,

                                                                                            ​




            descendants do not realize the coadjoint deformation-level action. main
            This is devastating for the advertised closed cotangent BF comparison. The best you
            currently have is:

            as a graded vector space / PBW special-fibre label set, not as an h-module, not as a
            Lie algebra representation, and not as a deformation-compatible boundary sector.
            Your principal-part repair is mathematically natural, but it is not part of the open
            polynomial brane theory. The paper admits it must be promoted to a factorization object
            before it can participate in the full cotangent lift. main
            So the descendant part of the theorem should be phrased as a basis-level
            identification only. Anything stronger is false.

            5. The “central operation” theorem is too close to tautological
            Theorem 0.2.17 constructs an interval-wise operation by multiplication with
                                                            ∫ a(t) Tr f (ϕ1 (t), ϕ2 (t)) dt.
                                                                 ​           ​             ​

            But in the reduced open model the observable algebra is graded-commutative, so
            multiplication by any closed element is automatically an ordinary Hochschild central
            operation. The paper itself says the proof uses Qϕi = 0, graded-commutativity, and
            then the Poisson identity after projection. main
                                                                                       ​




            So the ordinary E1-centrality part is not evidence of a closed-open theorem. The only
            nontrivial part is the Poisson bracket identity, and that identity is degree-zero, quotient-

            dependent, and not a full P0 factorization-center map.

            of closed-open string theory.
            6. The “sector” is selected by hand
            The open Hamiltonian algebra is defined as the sector generated by:
             1. nonempty primitive degree-zero traces;
             2. nonconstant primitive one-ψ Koszul classes.
            Then you exclude:
             1. the scalar trace Tr(1) = N ;
             2. Tr(ψ);
             3. all higher-ψ primitive homology;
             4. finite-N trace identities;
             5. the genuine coadjoint action mismatch.
            The draft is honest that “sector” is literal and that higher-ψ homology lies outside the
            sector. main
            But then the introduction and theorem language still make it sound like the open brane
            algebra itself is being matched to the closed Koszul dual. It is not. You are matching a
            deliberately carved-out subquotient/subsector.

            7. The large-N limit is algebraic, not physical
            Your stable large-N limit is degreewise invariant theory under block restriction. That is a
            valid algebraic stabilization. But it is not the physical large-N limit used in matrix models
            unless you also specify:
                                                                                    1
                                                             Tr       versus          Tr,
                                                                                       ​




                                                                                    N
            connected correlators/cumulants, scaling of ℏ, planar versus nonplanar terms, and the
            fate of central terms like
                                                             {Tr ϕ1 , Tr ϕ2 } = N .
                                                                       ​        ​




            Right now “connected stable trace sector” is doing several jobs at once: removing the
            empty trace, selecting primitive single traces, killing constants, and evading finite-rank
            trace identities. Those are not the same operation physically.
            You need a separate definition:
                             Primst ,    ​          ConnN →∞ ,    ​        Hamiltonian scalar quotient,

            and you should not conflate them.
            8. The reduced gauge/BV model suppresses a real quotient-stack
            issue
            You say you take GLN -invariants in characteristic zero, so the Chevalley part of gauge
            BRST acts trivially on trace functions. That is fine for trace functions, but it does not by
                                                ​




            itself identify the full BV quotient with the invariant Koszul complex.
            There are two different models hiding here:
              1. Algebraic quotient by a linearly reductive group, where taking invariants is exact.
https://chatgpt.com/c/69efa84c-a760-83ea-ae70-183a06ecd2d3                                                  6/261
28/04/2026, 17:50                                                        Whitepaper Critical Analysis

             2. Lie-algebra/BRST Chevalley-Eilenberg quotient, where gauge ghosts can have
                 their own cohomology unless a precise presentation kills them.
            Your Remark 0.2.67 tries to justify this, but the main calculation uses the reduced
            invariant complex as if the quotient-stack subtleties were automatically absent. That is
            acceptable only if you explicitly state:
                We are computing the algebraic invariant functions on the derived commuting
                scheme, not the full CE/BRST cohomology of the infinitesimal gauge algebra.
            Otherwise a referee can object that “the Chevalley part acts trivially on trace functions”
            is not the same as “the Chevalley sector has disappeared.”
            9. The one-ψ homology proof is plausible but under-proved
            Proposition 0.2.28 is one of the technically interesting parts of the paper. But the proof
            leans heavily on the chip-moving state complex and an Abel-map argument. The draft
            says the quotient state complex has the homology of S 1, with convex fibres and affine
            stabilizer quotients. main
            That is the kind of argument that will get attacked unless made completely formal. The
            danger points are:
             1. the passage from cyclic words with graded signs to cellular chains;
             2. the quotient by cyclic relabelling;
             3. stabilizers of configurations with symmetry;
             4. compatibility of orientations/signs with the two-ψ boundary;
             5. the claim that higher cells do not affect H1;
             6. the identification of the particular generator with Ψk,l .
                                                                              ​




                                                                                               ​




            The computational script checks up to small degree, but that does not replace the proof.
                    main

            If this proposition is essential, give it a standalone, fully combinatorial proof, or relegate
            it to a conjectural/computational lemma. Right now it is probably the most vulnerable
            purely algebraic proof in the paper.
            10. The Tate/Koszul-duality formalism is under-specified
            The claim
                                                              ∙

            for a completed Tate Lie algebra is believable, but the draft’s Lemma 0.2.40 is doing a
            huge amount of foundational work. A hostile reader will ask:
             1. What exact category of complete filtered Tate spaces is being used?
             2. What are the admissible quasi-isomorphisms?
             3. Is the CE coalgebra genuinely conilpotent after coefficient completion?
             4. Which completed bar/cobar adjunction is being invoked?

            You gesture at these, but not enough to make the theorem mechanically checkable.

            11. The closed sector is a formal BF model, not yet a physical closed
            string sector
            The paper distinguishes itself from Gwilliam–Williams and says it is not their
            holomorphic bosonic string. Good. But it still uses phrases like “mixed holomorphic-
            topological strings,” “twisted M-theory,” “closed string sector,” and “brane coupling.”
            The actual constructed object is a formal local Hamiltonian cotangent BF theory on
                                                                  R2 × C2

            with coefficient Lie algebra
                                                             h = C[[z1 , z2 ]]/C.
                                                              ​        ​     ​




            That is a perfectly reasonable BV toy model. But the physics origin is not derived. In
            particular:
             1. No parent 11-dimensional M-theory background is specified.
             2. The dimension count is not explained.
             3. The twist is not constructed.
             4. The brane boundary condition/defect theory is not derived from a worldvolume
                 theory.
             5. No anomaly cancellation/QME theorem is proved.
             6. No propagator or defect kernel is constructed.
             7. The quantum graph realization is explicitly left open.
            So the physics claim should be downgraded from “this is a local mixed string model” to:
https://chatgpt.com/c/69efa84c-a760-83ea-ae70-183a06ecd2d3                                            8/261
28/04/2026, 17:50                                                     Whitepaper Critical Analysis


               This is a formal local BV model motivated by the Hamiltonian sector expected in a
               mixed holomorphic-topological brane setup.
            That wording is much harder to attack.
            12. The BCOV/Kodaira-Spencer analogy is dangerous
            You describe the closed sector as Hamiltonian Kodaira-Spencer/BF. But the actual
            construction is not BCOV theory on a Calabi-Yau threefold, and not a direct truncation of
            BCOV. You use divergence-free vector fields on a holomorphic symplectic surface,
            identify them locally with Hamiltonians modulo constants, and then add a cotangent BF
            partner.
            That is mathematically coherent, but the phrase “Kodaira-Spencer” invites the wrong
            comparison. In BCOV, the field complex, divergence operator, anomaly structure, and
            quantization problem are much more rigid. Here the Hamiltonian reduction is a chosen
            local sector.
            I would use “Hamiltonian BF theory for the formal symplectic disk” as the primary name,
            and mention Kodaira-Spencer only as motivation.
            13. The quantum section is a target, not a result
            The Weyl/Moyal formulas are correct as algebraic deformation-quantization targets for
            the constant Poisson disk. But the draft is clear that the actual quantum boundary
            theorem is not proved. Proposition 0.2.52 only proves BRST descent of individual Weyl-
            ordered traces; the Moyal commutator identity in quantum Hamiltonian reduction is left
            as Problem 0.2.54. The draft also identifies the normal-ordering/Capelli shift
                                                             Y X − XY + ℏN I = 0

            as an obstruction that can feed lower-degree traces into the connected sector. main
            This is not a small technical issue. It is exactly where the classical trace-bracket story
            can fail quantum mechanically.
            So any sentence suggesting that the open quantum brane algebra is the Weyl/Moyal
            algebra should be changed to:
                    The Weyl/Moyal algebra is the proposed formal target; the reduced finite-N and
                    stable connected identities remain open.
https://chatgpt.com/c/69efa84c-a760-83ea-ae70-183a06ecd2d3                                               9/261
28/04/2026, 17:50                                                               Whitepaper Critical Analysis

            Your draft mostly says this, but the abstract and introduction should be ruthlessly
            consistent.
            14. The central extension is physically meaningful, not disposable
            bookkeeping
            Classically,
                                                                 {z1 , z2 } = 1
                                                                        ​        ​




            becomes zero in Aˉ, because constants are removed. But on the brane,
                                                             {Tr ϕ1 , Tr ϕ2 } = N .
                                                                    ​                 ​




            You remove this by projecting out scalar trace classes. Algebraically that is allowed for
            the reduced Hamiltonian vector-field algebra. Physically it is not innocent: it removes the
            center-of-mass canonical pair of the brane stack.
            This same issue reappears quantum mechanically as the normal-ordering shift. So the
            central term is not just a nuisance; it is the obstruction that keeps returning.
            I would make this a named obstruction:
               Scalar Hamiltonian / center-of-mass anomaly.
            Then every theorem should state whether it is before or after killing it.
            15. The figures weaken the paper
            The schematic ovals on pages 41, 50, and 51 do not communicate mathematical data:
            no labels, no propagator convention, no orientation, no automorphism factor, no
            boundary ordering, no kernel. The captions say they are not Feynman-integral proofs.
            That makes them look ornamental.
            Either remove them or replace them with real graph notation:
                                 Γ1 ,​     Γ3 ,​     Aut(Γ),      P∂ ,      ​        ordered boundary inputs.

            As drawn, they invite the accusation that the graph discussion is gestural.

            There are malformed citation labels in the body, for example things like “[13]razmyslov”
            and “[2]tsygan.” The PBW discussion appears to cite “[16]loday-vallette,” but [16] is

            Where the one-ψ descendants enter

            Your current draft already has the ingredients: the mixed local model, the open ghost-

            1. The Dirac principle of the paper
            A local theory is not primarily a Lagrangian. It is a rule assigning observables to regions.
https://chatgpt.com/c/69efa84c-a760-83ea-ae70-183a06ecd2d3                                                               23/261
28/04/2026, 17:50                                                                           Whitepaper Critical Analysis

            If U is a region, write
                                                                                    Obs(U )

            for the cochain complex of measurements supported in U . If
                                                                       U1 , … , Un ⊂ V
                                                                                ​                ​




            are disjoint, measurements in the Ui may be performed independently and then
            regarded as one measurement in V . This gives the structure map
                                                                           ​




                                              Obs(U1 ) ⊗ ⋯ ⊗ Obs(Un ) ⟶ Obs(V ).
                                                             ​                                           ​




            This is the factorization product. No category theory is being imposed from outside. It is
            just the algebraic expression of independent local experiments.
            If the theory is topological in a direction, moving an insertion in that direction does not
            change its physical class. Infinitesimally this means
                                                                               Lv = [Q, ιv ].
                                                                                        ​            ​




            Thus translations are Q-exact. Factorization is then locally constant in that direction.
            If the theory is holomorphic in a complex direction, antiholomorphic translations are Q-
            exact:
                                                                     L∂/∂ zˉi = [Q, ι∂/∂zˉi ].
                                                                                    ​
                                                                                        ​                        ​




            Thus the theory is not local in the Lorentzian sense. It is local in the operational sense:
            observables have supports, independent supports multiply, and motion in the
            topological or antiholomorphic directions is homotopically invisible.
            This should be the first-principles origin of factorization algebras in the paper.

            3. The basic closed-open measurement
            A closed Hamiltonian f (z1, z2) is measured by the brane by substituting the brane’s
            matrix-valued normal coordinates:
                                                     ​       ​




                                                                  JN (f ) = Tr f (ϕ1 , ϕ2 ).
                                                                        ​                              ​               ​




            At finite N one must choose an ordering. In the BV cohomology, adjacent swaps are
            exact because
                                                         Q Tr(ψvu) = Tr([ϕ1 , ϕ2 ]vu).                     ​               ​




            Thus the ordering ambiguity disappears after imposing the constraint. In the stable
            connected limit,
                                                                    J(f ) = Tr f (ϕ1 , ϕ2 )        ​           ​




            is a well-defined Hamiltonian observable.
            The matrix Poisson bracket gives
                                                         {J(f ), J(g)}open = J({f , g}h )  ​                                       ​




            after removal of the scalar Hamiltonian. This is not a mysterious string duality. It is the
            statement that the probe brane is a representation of the Hamiltonian algebra of the
            normal symplectic disk.
            For monomials,
                                                                 f = z1k z2l ,  ​   ​          g = z1m z2n ,       ​           ​




            one obtains

            4. Why the factorization center is forced
https://chatgpt.com/c/69efa84c-a760-83ea-ae70-183a06ecd2d3                                                                                     26/261
28/04/2026, 17:50                                                                                 Whitepaper Critical Analysis

            A closed insertion near the brane should define an operation on open insertions. If the
            closed insertion is moved past an open insertion, no physical change should occur
            except for controlled contact terms. Therefore a closed observable does not merely
            define an element of the open algebra. It defines a central operation on the open
            factorization algebra.
            For a locally constant open theory on a line, central operations are Hochschild cochains.
            Classically, because the open theory has a Poisson bracket, one must retain the Poisson
            compatibility. Thus the target is not the ordinary center but the derived P0-center:                                          ​




                                                                     P0
                                                                    Zfact (Obsopen ).
                                                                              ​




                                                                                  ​                               ​




            This is the correct physical object.
            The ordinary statement
                                                                  f ↦ Tr f (ϕ1 , ϕ2 )                     ​           ​




            only sees multiplication by a function. The derived center also sees vector fields and
            higher polyvectors. Those extra operations are exactly what the closed CE differential
            demands.
            This is the point to emphasize: the CE obstruction disappears only when closed fields
            are allowed to act as operations, not merely as central functions.

            7. Locality and the places where locality changes meaning
https://chatgpt.com/c/69efa84c-a760-83ea-ae70-183a06ecd2d3                                                                                                  30/261
28/04/2026, 17:50                                                          Whitepaper Critical Analysis

            The paper should be explicit that there are three different notions of locality.
            First, there is support locality along the brane. If two open measurements are
            supported in disjoint intervals, they multiply independently. Their bracket has a delta
            function, so it vanishes unless the supports meet. This is ordinary canonical locality in
            one dimension.
            Second, there is topological locality. Since translations in the topological directions are
            Q-exact,

                                                                Lv = [Q, ιv ],
                                                                   ​                ​




            the precise position of an insertion is not physical. Only the collision pattern of insertions
            matters. That is why the factorization algebra is locally constant.
            Third, there is formal holomorphic locality. The theory has been completed at the
            brane point p ∈ C2. It is not a theory of finite propagation through C2. It is a theory of
            holomorphic jets at p. Antiholomorphic translations are Q-exact, and holomorphic
            dependence is formal.
            The cotangent/principal-part sector is local in this formal sense. A principal part such as
                                                             z1−a−1 z2−b−1 dz1 dz2
                                                                       ​       ​        ​   ​




            is not a smooth function spread through the normal plane. It is a residue functional
            supported at the brane. Physically it is a transverse delta-current, or derivative of a
            delta-current, at the defect.
            Thus the paper should say:
             The cotangent boundary sector is distributionally local, not polynomially local.                ​




            This is not a defect of the model. It is what one expects for momenta or dual fields
            attached to a brane.
            Trying to realize the coadjoint module by ordinary polynomial descendants is like trying
            to realize momentum as a function of position. The correct realization is by local duals,
            principal parts, or polyvector operations.

            8. The role of the one-ψ descendants

            9. Unitarity
            The paper should not pretend that this local twisted model is unitary in the ordinary
            sense.
            It is not.
            The model is complex, BV, ghost-valued, and topological-holomorphic. It has no
            Lorentzian time, no positive Hamiltonian, no Hilbert space with positive inner product,
            and no reflection positivity statement. The variables include ghosts and antifields. A BV
            complex is not a unitary Hilbert space.
            The correct consistency conditions are instead:
                                                                          1
                                                                      QI + {I, I} = 0
                                                                          2
                                                                                        ​




            classically, and
                                                                 1
                                                             QI + {I, I} + ℏΔI = 0
                                                                 2
                                                                            ​




            quantum mechanically.
            In words:
                                         Classical consistency is the master equation.                                     ​




             Quantum consistency is anomaly cancellation plus factorization/OPE associativity



https://chatgpt.com/c/69efa84c-a760-83ea-ae70-183a06ecd2d3                                                                     33/261
28/04/2026, 17:50                                                                    Whitepaper Critical Analysis

            If a larger untwisted theory exists and is unitary, this local model may be its protected
            twisted sector. But the local sector itself does not remember ordinary unitarity. It
            remembers BRST cohomology, Ward identities, and deformation quantization.
            The right sentence is:
               We do not impose unitarity on a theory in which time translations have been made
               cohomologically trivial. The replacement for unitarity in the present local sector is the
               BV master equation and the associativity of the resulting factorization algebra.
            That is the honest physical position.

            10. How the paper should sound
            Here is an insertable opening in the intended tone.

            Local measurements and constraints.
            The object of study is a local constrained system. The normal plane to the brane is a
            formal holomorphic symplectic plane with coordinates z1, z2. Its infinitesimal canonical
            transformations are Hamiltonians modulo constants. A stack of N probes represents
                                                                                                                 ​       ​




            the two normal coordinates by matrices ϕ1, ϕ2. The symplectic potential is therefore
                                                                             ​               ​




                                                                      Tr(ϕ1 dϕ2 ),   ​               ​




            and invariance under change of basis of the probes imposes the first-class constraint
                                                                      [ϕ1 , ϕ2 ] = 0.
                                                                         ​               ​




            The gauge field A is the multiplier for this constraint. Thus the open action is forced:
                                                    S∂ = ∫ Tr(ϕ1 dϕ2 + A[ϕ1 , ϕ2 ]).
                                                         ​       ​               ​               ​           ​       ​




                                                             R

            The BV field ψ = A∗ records the constraint by
                                                                     Qψ = [ϕ1 , ϕ2 ].            ​       ​




            This is Dirac reduction written as a differential.

28/04/2026, 17:50                                                                                            Whitepaper Critical Analysis

            A closed Hamiltonian f is observed by the brane by evaluation on the probe
            coordinates,
                                                             f (z1 , z2 ) ⟼ Tr f (ϕ1 , ϕ2 ).
                                                                       ​            ​                                           ​           ​




            This is not yet the closed-open map. It is its degree-zero moment-map shadow. The full
            closed-open operation must assign to a closed local observable a central operation on
            all open local observables. Therefore its natural target is the derived Poisson
            factorization center.

            The center.
            Let h = C[[z1, z2]]/C be the Hamiltonian Lie algebra of the formal symplectic disk. In
            the stable connected sector the open Hamiltonian algebra is
                                  ​       ​




                                                                                    A∂ = S(h),
                                                                                             ​




            with Poisson bracket
                                                                       {Of , Og } = O{f ,g} .
                                                                                        ​                ​                          ​




            The derived P0-center of A∂ is the Poisson cochain complex
                                      ​                  ​




                                                      Z P0 (A∂ ) ≃ (PV(A∂ ), [π∂ , −]).
                                                               ​




                                                                               ​                                        ​               ​




            The closed Hamiltonian BF sector is the shifted cotangent Lie algebra
                                                                                   g = h ⋉ h∨ [1].

            Its local observables are
                                                                                             ∙
                                                                                            CCE (g).         ​




            There is a canonical isomorphism
                                                        ∙

            If cI is the CE coordinate dual to eI ∈ h, and uI is the CE coordinate dual to the shifted

                                                                           ​                                       ​

https://chatgpt.com/c/69efa84c-a760-83ea-ae70-183a06ecd2d3                                                                                          35/261
28/04/2026, 17:50                                            Whitepaper Critical Analysis

            Thus a closed Hamiltonian ghost acts as an infinitesimal operation on open observables,
            while the cotangent coordinate gives the boundary Hamiltonian function. This is the
            closed-open map.

            Locality.
            The factorization structure is the algebra of independent local measurements. If
            measurements are supported in disjoint intervals, they multiply. If the intervals move in
            the topological direction without collision, the motion is Q-exact and changes nothing in
            cohomology. If two insertions collide, the equal-time Poisson bracket gives the contact
            term.
            In the holomorphic normal direction the theory is formal. It is a theory of jets at the
            brane point. Coadjoint modes are principal parts, hence distributions supported at the
            brane. This is local in the sense appropriate to a defect: the support is on the defect,
            while the transverse behavior is encoded by residues.

            Unitarity.
            The model is a twisted BV sector. It is not a Lorentzian unitary theory. Its consistency
            condition is not positivity of a Hilbert space inner product, but the classical and quantum
            master equations. If the model is obtained from a unitary parent theory, unitarity belongs
            to the parent. The local sector retains only the cohomological algebra of protected
            observables.

            11. The actual thesis sentence
            The paper’s thesis should be something like:
               A stack of branes is a system of probes for the formal symplectic normal disk.
                   Dirac reduction of the probe phase space gives the open trace algebra.
             Hamiltonian BF theory is the shifted cotangent theory of canonical transformation
                The closed observables are precisely the derived Poisson central operations
                              on the stable open Hamiltonian brane algebra.

            This makes the factorization algebra unavoidable. It is not a technical language added
            after the physics. It is the local algebra of measurements in a constrained canonical
            system.

            1. The physical starting point: local measurements, not
            global strings

            full global worldsheet string theory with all backgrounds, moduli, amplitudes, and
            anomaly data. It studies the local operator algebra near a brane.
            A local field theory should assign to every region U a complex of observables
                                                                       Obs(U ).

            If U1, … , Un ⊂ V are disjoint, measurements supported in the Ui can be performed
            independently and then regarded as a measurement in V . This gives maps

            That is the physical meaning of a factorization algebra.
            If the theory is topological in a real direction, then moving an insertion in that direction is
            invisible in cohomology:
                                                                     Lv = [Q, ιv ].
                                                                            ​            ​




            So local observables are locally constant in that direction.
            If the theory is holomorphic in a complex direction, then antiholomorphic translations are

            3. Global versus formal-local Hamiltonians
            Globally, on a holomorphic symplectic surface X , not every symplectic vector field is
            globally Hamiltonian.
            A vector field v is symplectic if
                                                                  αv = −ιv ω
                                                                     ​                    ​




            is a closed holomorphic one-form. It is Hamiltonian only if there exists a holomorphic
            function f with
                                                                   df = αv .          ​




            So the obstruction to being globally Hamiltonian is a period class in
                                                                  H 1 (X, C).

            The paper isolates the formal local situation. On a formal disk, the holomorphic Poincaré
            lemma kills this obstruction. Every closed holomorphic one-form is exact, and every
            symplectic vector field is Hamiltonian modulo constants.
            That is why the local Hamiltonian algebra is clean:
                                                             h = C[[z1 , z2 ]]/C.
                                                              ​                   ​   ​




            Darboux coordinates are not canonical, but different choices differ by a formal
            symplectomorphism. The construction is therefore coordinate-independent up to the
            natural action of the formal symplectomorphism group. main

            7. The Dirac interpretation of the open action
            The term
                                                                                  ∫ Tr(ϕ1 dϕ2 )                                   ​                   ​




            means that ϕ1 and ϕ2 are canonically conjugate matrix coordinates. The symplectic
            form is
                                  ​           ​




                                                                 ΩN = Tr(dϕ1 ∧ dϕ2 ).
                                                                              ​                                                       ​                                   ​




            Thus
                                                                 {(ϕ1 )ij , (ϕ2 )kl } = δli δjk ,
                                                                                  ​               ​               ​           ​                               ​                   ​




            and
                                           {(ϕ1 )ij , (ϕ1 )kl } = 0,
                                                   ​   ​         ​    ​                                                               {(ϕ2 )ij , (ϕ2 )kl } = 0.
                                                                                                                                                          ​           ​                   ​   ​




            The field A is a Lagrange multiplier. Its equation of motion is
                                                                                          [ϕ1 , ϕ2 ] = 0.
                                                                                                      ​               ​




            This is the moment-map equation for simultaneous conjugation by GLN .                                                                                                                         ​




            For ϵ ∈ glN , the moment map component is
                              ​




                                                                     μϵ = − Tr(ϵ[ϕ1 , ϕ2 ]).
                                                                          ​                                                                   ​                   ​




            Its Hamiltonian flow is
                                                                                  δϵ ϕi = [ϵ, ϕi ].
                                                                                              ​               ​                                   ​




            So the open phase space is the Dirac reduction
                                                                     {[ϕ1 , ϕ2 ] = 0}/GLN .
                                                                                      ​                   ​                                                                   ​




            In BV language, the constraint is imposed by introducing the antifield
https://chatgpt.com/c/69efa84c-a760-83ea-ae70-183a06ecd2d3                                                                                                                                                    45/261
28/04/2026, 17:50                                                                                    Whitepaper Critical Analysis

                                                                                        ψ = A∗

            with differential
                                                                             Qψ = [ϕ1 , ϕ2 ],                                ​           ​




                                                                        Qϕ1 = Qϕ2 = 0.
                                                                                ​                                                ​




            So the reduced pointwise open BV algebra is
                                                    RN = C[(ϕ1 )ij , (ϕ2 )ij ] ⊗ Λ((ψ)ij ),
                                                             ​                      ​        ​                           ​           ​                 ​




            with
                                                                             Qψ = [ϕ1 , ϕ2 ].                                ​           ​




            This is exactly Dirac reduction written homologically.

            8. Local operators and the de Rham jet contraction
            Because the brane direction is topological, positive jets along the brane line are killed in
            cohomology.
            On the jet algebra, for a coordinate t along the brane,
                                                                             [dR , ι∂t ] = ∂t .
                                                                                        ​


                                                                                                     ​
                                                                                                         ​                               ​




            This gives an Euler-type contraction of positive jet degree. Therefore every local
            cohomology class has a representative depending only on field values at the insertion
            point:
                                                                 ϕ 1 (t 0 ),
                                                                    ​    ​                  ϕ 2 (t 0 ),
                                                                                                 ​                   ​                       ψ(t0 ),
                                                                                                                                                  ​




            not on derivatives.
            That is why the local open operator calculation reduces to the finite-dimensional
            invariant BV algebra
                                                                                 GLN
                                                                               (RN   , Q).                   ​

            one ψ around the trace gives no sign if it passes even letters, but two ψ’s anticommute.

            10. Adjacent swaps become Q-exact
            The differential is
                                                             Qψ = [x, y] = xy − yx.

            Therefore
                                                    Q Tr(ψvu) = Tr((xy − yx)vu).

            By cyclicity,
                                                Q Tr(ψvu) = Tr(uxyv) − Tr(uyxv).

                                                             Tr(uxyv) − Tr(uyxv)

                                                                               Tr(xk y l ).

            14. The scalar central subtlety
            Before quotienting constants, the simplest bracket is
                                                               {Tr ϕ1 , Tr ϕ2 } = N .
                                                                              ​            ​




            But in the reduced Hamiltonian algebra,
                                                            {z1 , z2 } = 1 ≡ 0

                                                                   {Of , Og } = O{f ,g}Aˉ
                                                                          ​       ​


                                                                                                          ​

            is true only after projecting out the scalar trace class.
            This is not a minor convention. It is the scalar Hamiltonian anomaly or center-of-mass
            central term. It reappears quantum mechanically as a Capelli/normal-ordering shift.
            So the corrected statement is:
             {Of , Og }open = O{f ,g}Aˉ
                     ​     ​       ​


                                                    ​
                                                        ​   in the connected Hamiltonian quotient by scalar trace clas

            Without that quotient, the formula fails for f = z1, g = z2.                           ​              ​

            17. Why principal parts are necessary
            Now we come to the principal-parts note.
            The continuous dual of
                                                                       h = C[[z1 , z2 ]]/C        ​                   ​




            is not best thought of as abstract symbols δa,b . Geometrically, it is realized by principal
            parts of meromorphic top forms.
                                                                                                              ​




            Define
                                 ρa,b = z1−a−1 z2−b−1 dz1 ∧ dz2 ,
                                       ​                ​      ​           ​              ​                                           a, b ≥ 0,                            a + b > 0.

            Let
                                                                       P = ⨁ C ρa,b .                     ​                                    ​




                                                                                    a,b≥0
                                                                                    a+b>0                 ​




            The residue pairing is
                                 ⟨ρa,b , z1m z2n ⟩ = Res0 (z1m−a−1 z2n−b−1 dz1 dz2 ) = δa,m δb,n .
                                               ​    ​                  ​                      ​                                            ​           ​       ​                ​   ​




            Equivalently, integrating over a small torus ∣z1∣ = ϵ1, ∣z2∣ = ϵ2,                        ​                                ​           ​                   ​




                                                          1
                                                              2
                                                                ∫ ∫ ρa,b z1m z2n = δa,m δb,n .
                                                        (2πi)
                                                                   ​                  ​                           ​           ​                            ​       ​

28/04/2026, 17:50                                                                          Whitepaper Critical Analysis

            Thus P identifies with
                                                                                h∨cont .       ​




            The exclusion

                                                                          ​        ​                       ​                   ​       ​




            which pairs with the constant 1. Since constants were removed from h, their dual must

            as the correct geometric dual, realized by brane-localized residue currents.

            18. Principal parts carry the coadjoint action
            The Hamiltonian action on principal parts is
                                                                         f ⋅ ρ = πpp {f , ρ},          ​




            where πpp projects a Laurent two-form to its principal-part component.
                            ​




            For
                                                                                             p q
                                                                              f = z1 z2 ,          ​           ​




            and
                                                                 ρa,b = z1−a−1 z2−b−1 dz1 dz2 ,
                                                                     ​                 ​                               ​           ​       ​




            one computes
                                         z1p z2q ⋅ ρa,b = −(pb − qa + p − q)ρa−p+1,b−q+1 ,
                                             ​   ​           ​                                                                                 ​




            with negative-index targets set to zero.
https://chatgpt.com/c/69efa84c-a760-83ea-ae70-183a06ecd2d3                                                                                         57/261
28/04/2026, 17:50                                                                                         Whitepaper Critical Analysis

            This is exactly the coadjoint action because residue integration by parts gives
                                                                    ⟨f ⋅ ρ, g⟩ = −⟨ρ, {f , g}⟩.

            That is the defining property of the coadjoint representation.
            For the linear Hamiltonians, the corrected formulas are
                                                                    z1 ⋅ ρa,b = −(b + 1)ρa,b+1 ,
                                                                      ​                   ​                                          ​




                                                                    z2 ⋅ ρa,b = (a + 1)ρa+1,b .
                                                                          ​                   ​                                  ​




            So linear Hamiltonians act as raising operators on principal parts.
            This is important because the copied principal-parts note contains a sentence saying z1
            lowers indices on principal parts. That sentence is incorrect. The formula in the paper is
                                                                                                                                                 ​




            the correct one.

            19. Why polynomial descendants are not the coadjoint
            module
            The open one-ψ descendants Ψa,b have the stable primitive action      ​




                                               {Op,q , Ψa,b } = (pb − qa) Ψa+p−1,b+q−1 ,
                                                            ​                 ​                                                          ​




            where Ψa,b is the averaged version of Ψa,b .
                             ​                                                                        ​




            The closed coadjoint action is
                                         ad∨z1p z2q δa,b = −(pb − qa + p − q)δa−p+1,b−q+1 .
                                                ​   ​
                                                        ​       ​                                                                            ​




            These are not the same.
            For example,
                                                                                                      O1,0    ​




            acts on polynomial descendants by
                                                                                      Ψa,b ↦ b Ψa,b−1 .
                                                                                                  ​                     ​




            But z1 acts coadjointly on principal parts by
                     ​




                                                                     ρa,b ↦ −(b + 1)ρa,b+1 .
                                                                                      ​                                      ​




https://chatgpt.com/c/69efa84c-a760-83ea-ae70-183a06ecd2d3                                                                                           58/261
28/04/2026, 17:50                                                                                 Whitepaper Critical Analysis

            The direction is opposite.
            Therefore:
             Ψa,b identify with h∨ only as graded vector-space labels, not as the coadjoint modul
                    ​




            The polynomial descendants are PBW-special-fibre representatives. They are not the
            deformation-level realization of the cotangent BF module.
            The deformation-level realization is the principal-part module P .

            20. No ordinary polynomial boundary realization of
            principal parts
            The paper gives a simple obstruction.
            The linear Hamiltonians
                                                     O1,0 = Tr ϕ1 ,
                                                              ​                               ​        O0,1 = Tr ϕ2   ​               ​




            act on ordinary polynomial boundary observables by constant derivations:
                                                                          ∂ϕ 2 ,  ​
                                                                                      ​
                                                                                                     −∂ϕ1 .   ​
                                                                                                                  ​




            On any ordinary polynomial, such derivations are locally nilpotent. Apply them enough
            times and the polynomial becomes zero.
            But on principal parts,
                                                        O1,0 ⋅ ρa,b = −(b + 1)ρa,b+1 ,
                                                                  ​           ​                                                   ​




                                                             O0,1 ⋅ ρa,b = (a + 1)ρa+1,b .
                                                                      ​                   ​                                   ​




            These actions are not locally nilpotent. They raise the pole order forever.
            Local nilpotence is preserved under module isomorphism. Therefore no collection of
            ordinary polynomial boundary observables can realize the principal-part coadjoint
            module.
            That is the core mathematical reason the polynomial Ψa,b cannot be the true cotangent
            boundary field.

            22. The Dirac interpretation of principal parts
            This is the most important physical idea in the principal-parts note.
            In ordinary mechanics, position and momentum are not the same kind of object.
            Position can be multiplication by x. Momentum is
                                                                                     d
                                                                       −iℏ             .
                                                                                       ​




                                                                                    dx
            It is a derivation. It naturally acts on distributions; for example,
                                                                      d
                                                                        δ(x − x0 )
                                                                        ​                          ​




                                                                     dx
            is another distribution.
            Trying to realize momentum as an ordinary function of position is the wrong category.
            The same happens here.
            Hamiltonians
                                                                       f (z1 , z2 )
                                                                                ​          ​




            are holomorphic functions. Their duals are not another family of holomorphic functions.
            Their duals are residue currents:
                                                             ρa,b = z1−a−1 z2−b−1 dz1 dz2 .
                                                                 ​          ​                  ​       ​   ​




https://chatgpt.com/c/69efa84c-a760-83ea-ae70-183a06ecd2d3                                                         61/261
28/04/2026, 17:50                                                                    Whitepaper Critical Analysis

            They are holomorphic analogues of derivatives of delta-functions supported at the
            brane.
            That is why the brane cotangent sector must be distributional in the transverse
            holomorphic directions. A brane is a defect; defect-localized dual fields are naturally
            delta-currents normal to the defect.
            So the corrected physical slogan is:
             Hamiltonian modes are functions; cotangent modes are brane-supported residue cu

            24. Three notions of locality
            The documents distinguish three physical meanings of locality.
            24.1 Support locality along the brane
            On the brane line, observables have compact support.
            If two observables are supported in disjoint intervals, their product is independent. The
            equal-time bracket has a delta function:
                                                       {Of (a), Og (b)} = O{f ,g} (ab).
                                                             ​            ​                     ​




            The test functions multiply because the bracket is supported where the insertions
            collide.
            This is ordinary canonical locality.
            24.2 Topological locality
            Along the topological directions,
                                                                 Lv = [Q, ιv ].
                                                                      ​                ​




            Moving insertions does not change cohomology unless insertions collide. Therefore the
            factorization algebra is locally constant in those directions.
            This is why the brane line behaves like an E1-algebra after passing to cohomology.
                                                                               ​




            24.3 Formal holomorphic locality
            In the holomorphic normal directions, the model is completed at the brane point. It is a
            theory of formal holomorphic jets, not a theory of finite-speed propagation through C2.
https://chatgpt.com/c/69efa84c-a760-83ea-ae70-183a06ecd2d3                                                   63/261
28/04/2026, 17:50                                                                    Whitepaper Critical Analysis

            Antiholomorphic translations are Q-exact:
                                                                L∂/∂ zˉi = [Q, ι∂/∂zˉi ].
                                                                         ​
                                                                             ​                      ​




            The principal parts are local in this formal/distributional sense. They are residue currents
            supported at the brane, not smooth fields spread through C2.
            So the cotangent sector is:
                                        distributionally local transverse to the brane.                             ​




            25. Unitarity
            This model is not a Lorentzian unitary quantum field theory.
            It is complex, BV, ghost-valued, topological-holomorphic, and local/formal. It has no
            positive-definite Hilbert space built into it, no ordinary time-evolution unitarity, and no
            reflection positivity statement.
            The correct consistency condition is the classical master equation
                                                                    1
                                                                QI + {I, I} = 0,
                                                                    2
                                                                                 ​




            and quantum mechanically the quantum master equation
                                                                 1
                                                             QI + {I, I} + ℏΔI = 0.
                                                                 2
                                                                     ​




            So in this paper, “physical consistency” means:
             BV master equation + factorization/OPE associativity + anomaly cancellation if q

            If this model is a protected twisted sector of a larger unitary theory, unitarity belongs to
            the parent theory, not to the local twisted sector by itself.

            27. Quantum matrix reduction and the Capelli obstruction
            On the open side, quantizing
                                                                           ∫ Tr(ϕ1 dϕ2 )                           ​           ​




            gives the Weyl algebra generated by matrix entries
                                                                 X = ϕ1 ,              ​                               Y = ϕ2 ,                ​




            with
                                                                  [Xji , Ylk ] = ℏ δli δjk .
                                                                               ​                       ​                           ​       ​




            The quantum comoment for conjugation is normal ordered:
                                                                 μϵ = − Tr([ϵ, X]Y ).
                                                                   ​   ​




            It satisfies
                                                                   ℏ−1 [μϵ , a] = ϵ ⋅ a.   ​   ​




            The quantum brane algebra is the BRST quantum Hamiltonian reduction
                                                                  ∙
                                                   Obsqbrane,N = CBRST (glN , WN , μ).
                                                                           ​                                           ​               ​           ​   ​




            Weyl-ordered traces
                                                        JN (f ) = Tr OpW (f )(X, Y )
                                                             ​                                                             ​




            are invariant and descend through quantum Hamiltonian reduction.
https://chatgpt.com/c/69efa84c-a760-83ea-ae70-183a06ecd2d3                                                                                                 66/261
28/04/2026, 17:50                                                     Whitepaper Critical Analysis

            But this does not prove the full quantum Moyal identity. The obstruction is the normal-
            ordering shift:
                                                    μϵ = Tr(ϵ(Y X − XY + ℏN I)).
                                                       ​




            So the quantum moment relation is
                                                             Y X − XY + ℏN I = 0.

            Therefore
                                                Tr(AXY ) − Tr(AY X) = ℏN Tr(A)

            modulo the quantum moment ideal.
            This is a Capelli-type shift. It can feed lower-degree traces into the connected sector. A
            full quantum theorem must either cancel, renormalize, or correctly account for this shift.
            So the quantum part of the paper gives the algebraic Weyl/Moyal target, not a
            completed quantum closed-open theorem.

            30. Errata and corrections
            Here are the corrections I would make explicitly.
            1. Principal-part linear action
            The principal-parts note says, in one place, that acting by z1 lowers indices on principal
            parts. That is wrong.
                                                                                                                                 ​




            The correct formula is
                                                                 z1 ⋅ ρa,b = −(b + 1)ρa,b+1 ,
                                                                   ​             ​                                           ​




                                                                 z2 ⋅ ρa,b = (a + 1)ρa+1,b .
                                                                       ​             ​                               ​




https://chatgpt.com/c/69efa84c-a760-83ea-ae70-183a06ecd2d3                                                                               69/261
28/04/2026, 17:50                                                                                            Whitepaper Critical Analysis

            So linear Hamiltonians raise pole order on principal parts.
            2. Polynomial descendants do not simply “raise indices”
            The polynomial descendant action is
                                                     Op,q : Ψa,b ↦ (pb − qa)Ψa+p−1,b+q−1 .
                                                                 ​               ​                                                              ​




            Whether this raises, lowers, or preserves total degree depends on p + q:
                                                                 degtarget = a + b + p + q − 2.
                                                                                         ​




            Linear Hamiltonians lower total degree by one, quadratic Hamiltonians preserve total
            degree, and higher Hamiltonians raise it.
            The real point is not “raising versus lowering” in general. The real point is that the action
            is not the coadjoint action.
            3. The coadjoint action formula is correct in the paper
            The correct coadjoint/principal-part formula is
                                         z1p z2q ⋅ ρa,b = −(pb − qa + p − q)ρa−p+1,b−q+1 .
                                             ​       ​               ​                                                                              ​




            This should be treated as the reference formula.
            4. The smeared bracket formula needs the scalar quotient
            The formula
                                                     {I∂ (a, f ), I∂ (b, g)} = I∂ (ab, {f , g}Aˉ )
                                                             ​                               ​                         ​                    ​




            must be read in the connected Hamiltonian quotient by scalar trace classes.
            Otherwise, for f = z1, g = z2,       ​                       ​




                                                 {I∂ (a, z1 ), I∂ (b, z2 )} = N ∫ a(t)b(t) dt,
                                                         ​                   ​       ​               ​




            while
                                                                                     {z1 , z2 }Aˉ = 0.
                                                                                                 ​       ​       ​




            So the scalar central term must be projected out.

            3. The second serious inconsistency: Ψa,b → ρa,b cannot

                                                                                                                                   ​           ​

            The draft correctly distinguishes polynomial one-ψ descendants from principal parts. It

            4. The “interpolation” theorem is not yet a theorem
            The draft says the polynomial Ψa,b basis and the principal-part ρa,b basis are “two
            different bases of the same g-module,” interpolated by the Rees/Moyal parameter ℏ. But
                                                                   ​                                                ​




            the same section also says the PBW special-fibre map is not an h-module isomorphism
            and that the actions diverge explicitly. main
            Those two statements cannot both be literally true.
            If two bases are bases of the same h-module, the matrices of the action must be
            conjugate. But the polynomial action is locally nilpotent under linear Hamiltonians, while
            the principal-part action is not. Your own no-go theorem says ordinary polynomial
            boundary observables cannot realize the principal-part module precisely because local
            nilpotence is preserved under module isomorphism. main
            So the corrected statement should be:
                                 Ψa,b and ρa,b are not two bases of the same h-module.
                                        ​              ​                                                                ​




            They are two different realizations of the same label set or the same PBW/cotangent
            formal symbol set:
                                                                       Aˉdesc ≅ h∨cont
                                                                                ​                   ​




            as graded vector spaces, but not as h-modules.
            To make the interpolation claim real, you need to construct an actual ℏ-dependent
            module
                                                                            Mℏ            ​

            over a Rees/Weyl algebra, together with two specializations:

            and

            This is not in the draft yet. The natural candidate is a Fourier-Borel/Rees Dℏ -module at
            the brane:

            Then take a delta-module or local-cohomology module

            or its holomorphic local-cohomology realization

            The Hamiltonian vector fields act by Lie derivative. The principal parts are the ℏ = 0
            residue-current realization. The associated graded is a cotangent-fiber symbol module.
            If you can identify the polynomial Ψ-action as the Fourier/Borel transform of that

            5. The factorization algebra must use de Rham compact
            supports, not just Cc∞ (I)                              ​




            The paper wants locality along the brane line to be a factorization algebra statement.
            That is right. But several interval-wise definitions use
                                                                            hI = Cc∞ (I) ⊗ h
                                                                                        ​                               ​




https://chatgpt.com/c/69efa84c-a760-83ea-ae70-183a06ecd2d3                                                                                                              78/261
28/04/2026, 17:50                                                                       Whitepaper Critical Analysis

            as if this were locally constant under inclusions of intervals. It is not. There is no
            differential in Cc∞ (I), so inclusions of intervals are not quasi-isomorphisms.
                                       ​

                                                                    hI = Ω∙c (I)⊗h,
                                                                                ​        ​          ​       ​




            with differential ddR , and bracket
                                            ​




                                                     [α ⊗ f , β ⊗ g] = (α ∧ β) ⊗ {f , g}.

            Then compactly supported de Rham cohomology of an interval is one-dimensional in
            top degree, and extension by zero is the correct cosheaf operation. The degree-zero
            current formula
                                                    Bf (a) = ∫ a(t) Tr f (ϕ1 (t), ϕ2 (t)) dt
                                                       ​                ​                               ​           ​




                                                                    I

            is then the shadow of a top-degree compactly supported form
                                                                             a(t) dt ⊗ f .

            This resolves the physical locality correctly:
            support locality + topological de Rham contraction = locally constant factorization

            The draft already knows the de Rham contraction is essential, but the theorem
            statements should bake it into the definitions rather than add it afterward. main

            10. The chain-level primitive projection should be renamed
            The theorem currently says the primitive projection

https://chatgpt.com/c/69efa84c-a760-83ea-ae70-183a06ecd2d3                                                                            83/261

            The right name is:
                                                primitive Lie/P0 quotient projection
                                                                                 ​                                            ​




            not
                                                  cotangent factorization-center lift.

            A factorization algebra remembers products. If your quotient kills products of positive
            primitives, it is not the same algebraic object as the factorization algebra generated by
            those primitives. It is the indecomposable Lie shadow of that algebra.

            11. The physics can be made much stronger
            The paper should not sound like it is borrowing physics decorations from string theory. It
            should sound like it is deriving the structure from three physical principles.
            Principle 1: Dirac constrained probes
            The brane stack probes the formal symplectic disk. The normal coordinates become
            matrices:
                                                                           z i ⇝ ϕi .
                                                                             ​                        ​




            The symplectic potential is forced:
                                                              θN = Tr(ϕ1 dϕ2 ).
                                                                       ​                          ​           ​




            Conjugation invariance gives the moment map
                                                             μϵ = − Tr(ϵ[ϕ1 , ϕ2 ]).
                                                               ​                                          ​       ​




            The first-order action is therefore
                                                    S∂ = ∫ Tr(ϕ1 dϕ2 + A[ϕ1 , ϕ2 ]).
                                                         ​         ​                 ​        ​                       ​   ​




                                                              R

            The BV variable
                                                                           ψ = A∗

            records the constraint:
https://chatgpt.com/c/69efa84c-a760-83ea-ae70-183a06ecd2d3                                                                        84/261
28/04/2026, 17:50                                                                 Whitepaper Critical Analysis

                                                                      Qψ = [ϕ1 , ϕ2 ]. ​               ​




            This is not an analogy. It is Dirac reduction in BV form.
            Principle 2: Witten closed-open centrality
            A closed insertion near a brane is not merely a boundary value. It is a central operation
            on all open measurements. Therefore the target is not the open algebra but
                                                                       P0
                                                                      Zfact
                                                                          ​




                                                                            (Obsopen ).
                                                                              ​                    ​




            The trace
                                                                     f ↦ Tr f (ϕ1 , ϕ2 )   ​               ​




            is only the moment-map shadow.
            Principle 3: Cotangent fields are transverse currents
            The dual of a holomorphic Hamiltonian is not another holomorphic Hamiltonian. It is a
            residue current:
                                                             ρa,b = z1−a−1 z2−b−1 dz1 dz2 .
                                                                 ​                ​            ​               ​   ​




            This is the holomorphic analogue of the fact that momentum is not multiplication by a
            function but a distributional/derivative operation. The brane is a defect, so cotangent
            boundary modes are naturally transverse delta-currents.
            These three principles should be the first section. They make factorization algebra feel
            physically inevitable.
