            14. Replacement abstract
            Here is the abstract I would use:
               We construct a formal local closed-open model for a mixed holomorphic-topological
               brane on
                                                                                   R2 × C2

                    near a brane line R × {0}. The open ghost-zero theory is the Dirac constrained
                    matrix system
                                                             ∫ Tr(ϕ1 dϕ2 + A[ϕ1 , ϕ2 ]),
                                                                  ​                ​       ​               ​   ​




                                                              R

                    whose BV reduction is Qψ = [ϕ1, ϕ2]. The closed Hamiltonian sector is shifted
                    cotangent BF theory for the reduced Hamiltonian Lie algebra
                                                                       ​       ​




                                                                      h = C[[z1 , z2 ]]/C.     ​   ​




                    We prove that the closed CE algebra
                                                                       ∙
                                                                      CCE (h ⋉ h∨cont [1])
                                                                           ​                           ​




               is canonically isomorphic to the derived Poisson factorization center of the stable
               open Hamiltonian algebra S(h). Under this isomorphism, the CE coordinate dual to a
               Hamiltonian mode maps to a constant polyvector operation, while the CE coordinate
               dual to the shifted cotangent mode maps to the boundary trace Hamiltonian
               Tr f (ϕ1 , ϕ2 ). The continuous dual h∨cont is identified with the principal-part residue
               module supported at the brane, making the cotangent sector a distributional defect-
                              ​     ​                                                  ​




               local current. We separately compute the PBW special-fibre stable open descendant
               sector generated by the one-ψ Koszul classes and show why it is a graded shadow,
               not the deformation-level coadjoint module. Finally, we isolate the scalar U (1)
               center anomaly and formulate the all-order Weyl/Moyal quantum Hamiltonian
               reduction problem.
            This abstract is strong, not modest. It also avoids false equivalences.

            when they should be separated and then recomposed with explicit maps. main

            201. One-paragraph strongest-version vision
            The strongest conceivable version of this whitepaper is not a speculative string note. It
            is a theorem-driven Dirac-Witten local model: a brane stack is a constrained matrix
            probe of a formal symplectic disk; its stable Hamiltonian trace algebra is the open
            measurement algebra; the closed Hamiltonian BF theory is the shifted cotangent theory
            of canonical transformations; and the closed CE observables are exactly the derived
            Poisson central operations on the open algebra. The polynomial one-ψ descendants are
            the PBW-special-fibre shadow, while the true cotangent modes are principal-part
            residue currents supported at the defect. The scalar U (1) anomaly is the same class
            classically and quantum mechanically, and the degree-zero quantum sector is governed
            by the Weyl/Moyal deformation, with the full Costello graph realization isolated as the
            remaining analytic theorem.

            III. Resolutions of the seven named obligations
            You listed seven obligations. The clean paper should not merely say they remain open; it
            should either solve the reduced form, prove a no-go, or isolate the missing theorem so
            sharply that the direction is cleared.
            1. All-N radial-parts normalization
            Current status

            There are exactly three clean solutions. The paper should state them as alternatives.

                                                             Str(I) = N − N = 0.

            Therefore the scalar contact becomes
                                                             ℏ Str(I) ω(f , g) = 0.

            The scalar anomaly vanishes.
            This is the cleanest QME route, but it changes the brane stack.

            VI. Final structure of the platonic clean paper
           The ideal paper should have this table of contents:
            1. Three principles: Dirac, Witten, Grothendieck.
            2. Local mixed model and field content.
            3. Dirac brane probe theorem.
            4. Stable trace and one-ψ PBW shadow.
            5. Stratified Koszul duality: Layers 0–7.
            6. CE/PV derived P0-center theorem.
            7. Matlis principal-part cotangent theorem.
                                               ​




            8. Brane-line factorization currents.
            9. Unreduced cyclic-word principal-part centrality homotopy.
           10. Scalar U (1) anomaly and QME cancellation alternatives.
           11. Degree-zero Moyal/Weyl theorem.
           12. Radial-parts theorem: conditional or fully proved appendix.
           13. Reduced Wick graph theorem and Costello realization problem.
           14. Weighted Tate regulator and strict endpoint no-go.
           15. Cross-volume non-transfer theorem.
           16. Appendices: signs, Matlis, factorization currents, bubble-sort homotopy, Moyal
               coefficients, radial parts, QME obstruction, bibliography.

            Theorem A. Dirac brane probe
            Let

                                                     S∂ = ∫ Tr(ϕ1 dϕ2 + A[ϕ1 , ϕ2 ]).

                                                                     R

            2. Koszul duality as the theory of possible bulk-boundary
            couplings
            This is the new organizing content that should be inserted into the paper.

https://chatgpt.com/c/69efa84c-a760-83ea-ae70-183a06ecd2d3                                                                          222/261
28/04/2026, 17:50                                                                  Whitepaper Critical Analysis

            Koszul duality is not just a way to compare two algebras after they have already been
            built. In this setting, it is the type system for allowed couplings between bulk and
            boundary algebras.
            The closed algebra is
                                                                         ∙
                                                                    B = CCE (g).              ​




            The open algebra is a P0-factorization algebra
                                                  ​




                                                                A = Obscl
                                                                       open,H .                                       ​




            A classical closed-open coupling is not a map
                                                                      B → A.

            It is a map
                                                                       P0
                                                              κ : B ⟶ Zfact (A).                          ​




                                                                                                              ​           ​




            Since
                                                                         ∙
                                                                    B = CCE (g),              ​




            a map
                                                                     ∙
                                                                    CCE (g) → R​




            to a complete commutative dg algebra R is equivalent, under the usual CE/Maurer-
            Cartan dictionary, to a Maurer-Cartan element
                                                                    Θκ ∈ g ⊗R +
                                                                       ​                              ​           ​




            satisfying
                                                                  1
                                                             dΘκ + [Θκ , Θκ ] = 0.
                                                                  2
                                                                ​          ​          ​                       ​




            Taking
                                                                         P0
                                                                    R = Zfact (A)         ​




                                                                                                  ​




            says:
                                                                             P0
                      closed-open couplings are Maurer-Cartan elements in g⊗Zfact (A).                                        ​
                                                                                                                                  ​




                                                                                                                                      ​   ​

28/04/2026, 17:50                                                                                Whitepaper Critical Analysis

            Equivalently, by bar-cobar/Koszul duality,
                                                                                B ! ≃ U (g),

            so the same coupling is an action of
                                                                                            U (g)

            by derived central operations on A.
            Thus the coupling problem is:
             Find representations of the Koszul-dual closed enveloping algebra in the derived ce

            This is the precise algebraic form of the Witten closed-open principle.

            2.3 Coupling obstruction theory
            A proposed coupling
                                                                  ∙
                                                             κ : CCE (g) → Z P0 (A)
                                                                         ​
                                                                                                      ​




            can fail in exactly four ways.
            Obstruction 1: CE source obstruction
            Trying to send
                                                                         cI ↦ OI          ​




            fails because cI is not a closed length-one CE class. The Lie algebra h is perfect, so
            Hamiltonian CE coordinates are not closed.
            Resolution:
                                                             cI ↦ θ I ,                 uI ↦ O I .
                                                                                              ​              ​




            Obstruction 2: cotangent module obstruction
            Trying to use
                                                                             Ψa,b   ​




            as the coadjoint module fails because the h-action is wrong. The principal-part module
                                                                     P = h∨cont                   ​




https://chatgpt.com/c/69efa84c-a760-83ea-ae70-183a06ecd2d3                                                                                           226/261
28/04/2026, 17:50                                                                   Whitepaper Critical Analysis

            is forced.
            Resolution:
                                                             ρa,b = z1−a−1 z2−b−1 dz1 dz2 .
                                                                 ​                  ​           ​   ​     ​




            Obstruction 3: scalar central obstruction
            The scalar-reduced bracket kills
                                                                         {z1 , z2 } = 1,
                                                                                ​       ​




            but the brane bracket gives
                                                               {Tr ϕ1 , Tr ϕ2 } = N .
                                                                            ​               ​




            Resolution options:
             1. keep the scalar central extension;
             2. impose scalar reduction;
             3. cancel with supertrace;
             4. absorb by central character;
             5. add a scalar counterterm.
            Obstruction 4: analytic QME obstruction
            The formal algebraic derived center does not automatically give a Costello renormalized
            brane-defect QME solution.
            Resolution requires a brane-defect graph theorem with propagator, counterterms,
            anomaly cancellation, and centrality homotopies.

            4. Algorithms and procedures
            Algorithm 1. Dirac probe construction
            Input: formal symplectic disk (C20, ω = dz1 ∧ dz2), brane rank N .
                                                                   ​                                  ​                       ​




            Procedure:
             1. Replace
                                                                                 zi ↦ ϕi ∈ glN .
             2. Pull back the symplectic potential:
                                                                                          ​               ​                               ​




                                                                            θN = Tr(ϕ1 dϕ2 ).
             3. Compute conjugation moment map:
                                                                                      ​                                   ​                   ​




                                                                           μϵ = − Tr ϵ[ϕ1 , ϕ2 ].
             4. Write the first-order action:
                                                                             ​                                                    ​                   ​




                                                                            S∂ = ∫ θ N − μ A .
                                                                                  ​                               ​                               ​




             5. Introduce BV/Koszul field
                                                                                 Qψ = [ϕ1 , ϕ2 ].                     ​               ​




            Output: open BV algebra
                                                             RN = C[ϕ1 , ϕ2 ] ⊗ Λ(ψ).
                                                                       ​                          ​           ​




            Algorithm 2. Classical ordering-independence by bubble sort
            Input: a cyclic word w in x = ϕ1, y = ϕ2.          ​                              ​




            Goal: construct a chain homotopy between [w] and [xayb ].
            Procedure:
https://chatgpt.com/c/69efa84c-a760-83ea-ae70-183a06ecd2d3                                                                                                231/261
28/04/2026, 17:50                                                                                   Whitepaper Critical Analysis

             1. Choose a deterministic bubble-sort path
                                                              w = w 0 , w 1 , … , w r = xa y b .
             2. At step s, suppose
                                                                                       ​        ​                                ​




                                                        ws = As y xBs ,                                          ws+1 = As xyBs .
             3. Define
                                                          ​               ​                ​                                         ​               ​       ​

            Algorithm 3. Constructing Ψa,b                                         ​

            9. Final insertable master theorem
            Here is the theorem that should replace the current umbrella summary.
            Theorem. Local closed-open Hamiltonian center theorem.
            Let
                                                                     h = C[[z1 , z2 ]]/C ⋅ 1              ​         ​




            be the reduced Hamiltonian Lie algebra of the formal symplectic disk, and let

            10. One-paragraph final synthesis
            Koszul duality in this paper is not merely a comparison between a closed algebra and a
            large-N open algebra. It is the algebraic mechanism that classifies which bulk fields are
            allowed to couple to which boundary operations. A closed CE algebra CCE ∙
                                                                                       (g) can
            couple to the brane only by a map into the derived P0-center of the open algebra;
                                                                                                                        ​




            equivalently, by a Maurer-Cartan/twisting datum or by an action of the Koszul-dual
                                                                                                            ​




            enveloping algebra U (g) through central operations. In this type system, Hamiltonian
            bulk generators become vector-field operations, shifted cotangent CE coordinates
            become boundary Hamiltonian functions, Matlis principal parts become the
            deformation-correct cotangent currents, PBW descendants become only special-fibre
            labels, and the scalar U (1) class measures the obstruction to unreduced lifting. That is
https://chatgpt.com/c/69efa84c-a760-83ea-ae70-183a06ecd2d3                                                                  260/261
28/04/2026, 17:50                                                      Whitepaper Critical Analysis

            the conceptual heart of the clean paper: Koszul duality is the grammar of closed-open
            coupling.
